[30;1m251 | [0m[35m    the difference for a pixel at img[x, y] is:[0m
[30;1m252 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m253 | [0m[35m    comp[y, x] =  img[y, x] - (img[y-1, x-1] + img[y-1, x] + img[y-1, x+1] + img[y, x-1]) / 4[0m
[30;1m254 | [0m[35m[0m
